1) Regular Federal grants-in-aid include periodic Federal payments to State (territorial) and local governments for specified purposes. Three general categories of expenditures are excluded: (1) Grants financed from relief and recovery appropriations such as Public Works Administration grants and those for road and highway projects; (2) payments to individuals from regular and emergency appropriations such as agricultural conservation program, Works Projects Administration and Civilian Conservation Corps expenditures; and (3) direct Federal expenditures in cooperation with States such as those for the National Guard, the control of animal diseases, agricultural pest control and farm forestry extension work.
2) Amounts shown in column (3) do not include the following sums appropriated separately for the territories: Item 1b: Alaska, $23,750; Hawaii, $60,000; Puerto Rico, $45,000; Item 2a: Hawaii and Puerto Rico $121,165; Item 2c: Alaska, $21,418; Puerto Rico, $65,000; Items 6a-6c: Hawaii, $30,000; Puerto Rico, $105,000; Item 3: District of Columbia, $25,000; Puerto Rico, $15,000; Hawaii, $5,000.
3) $30,000 for each State and territory.
4) $50,000 for each State and territory.
5) Include Alaska, Hawaii and Puerto Rico.
6) Includes Hawaii.
7) None, but must meet matching requirements for Items 2a and 2b.
8) Includes Hawaii and Puerto Rico.
9) $1,988,940 of this amount allotted for payments to States and Hawaii.
10) Additional authorization to provide (as needed) $10,000 minimum allotment; $27,000 for Item 6a; $50,000 for Item 6b; and $90,000 for Item 6c.
11) $10,000 minimum allotment to each State.
12) Includes District of Columbia, Alaska, Hawaii and Puerto Rico.
13) Additional authorisation of $175,000 to provide (as needed) $20,000 minimum allotments for Items 7a-7c combined.
14) $20,000 minimum allotment to each State and territory.
15) Additional authorization of $54,000 to provide (as needed) $10,000 minimum allotment to each State and territory.
16) $10,000 minimum allotment to each State and territory.
17) $20,000 minimum allotment to each State and Puerto Rico.
18) Payments are made to American Printing House for the Blind for books and apparatus supplied to public institutions for the blind in the States, territories and District of Columbia.
19) Includes $10,000 representing interest on $250,000 permanent fund.
20) Includes Alaska, District of Columbia, Hawaii, Puerto Rico and Virginia.
21) Represents amount approved by Surgeon General for apportionment to States and territories from appropriation of $5,000,000.
22) Not exceeding $5,000,000 for 1940; not exceeding $7,000,000 for 1941; and thereafter such sums as may be required.

23/ Includes District of Columbia, Alaska and Hawaii.
24/ Appropriations for Items 12, 13, 14 may be transferred interchangeably with approval of the Bureau of the Budget.
25/ Sum sufficient to carry out purposes of title.
26/ Includes Alaska and Hawaii.
27/ Amounts Congress may deem necessary.
28/ $10,000 minimum allotment to each State, Alaska and Hawaii.
29/ The Federal Government matches appropriations made by States. The maximum is the amount allotted on the basis of population. Each State (including local governments) must provide as a minimum at least $5,000, and not less than 25 percent of its allotted share.
30/ Includes District of Columbia, Hawaii and Puerto Rico.
31/ 2-1/2 percent may be retained for administration and research.
32/ Authorizations for highway purposes are made for two-year periods and are available until expended. Appropriation for 1940 was made under authorization for 1939. Fiscal year 1940 authorizations are: Item 20, $100,000,000; Item 21, $15,000,000; Item 22, $20,000,000. Fiscal year 1941 authorizations are: Item 20, $115,000,000; Item 21, $15,000,000; Item 22, $30,000,000. $5,000,000 of amounts appropriated for highway purposes may be allotted to States for emergency repairs. Appropriations are authorized to reimburse regular highway aid funds for such expenditures.
33/ Minimum State share, 1/2 of 1 percent of total allotment.
34/ When a State contains unappropriated public lands and nontaxable Indian lands in excess of 5 percent of total area of State, Federal grant may exceed 50 percent of total cost of projects by a percentage equal to one-half the percentage of the State's area consisting of such lands.
35/ To States having more than 5 percent of their area in unappropriated public lands, nontaxable Indian lands or other Federal reservations, other than forest reservations.
36/ Maximum annual contribution = (project cost) x (going Federal interest rate + 1 percent).
37/ Grantee must contribute in cash, tax remissions or tax exemptions 20 percent of the amount of annual contributions.
38/ Proceeds of tax on firearms, shells and cartridges (29 I.R.C. 3407); 8 percent may be retained for administration.
39/ Maximum State share $150,000; minimum, $15,000 if State provides $5,000.
40/ For one school in each specified port. Schools are now being maintained in four of the specified ports.
41/ $90,000 for repair of vessels.
42/ Secretary of Navy may match funds, not to exceed $25,000 per school, and may furnish naval vessels and equipment.
43/ Amounts necessary are allotted from appropriations for Veterans' Administration. Allotment for fiscal year 1940, $1,149,000.
